CREATE INDEX idx_loyalty_offer_outputs_lp_cost 
            ON loyalty_offer_outputs(lp_cost)
        ;
DROP TABLE loyalty_offer_required_items;
CREATE TABLE loyalty_offer_requirements (
                offer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                required_type_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                required_quantity INTEGER NOT NULL,
                PRIMARY KEY (offer_id, required_type_id)
            );
CREATE INDEX idx_loyalty_offer_requirements_offer_id 
            ON loyalty_offer_requirements(offer_id)
        ;
CREATE INDEX idx_loyalty_offer_requirements_type_id 
            ON loyalty_offer_requirements(required_type_id)
        ;
DROP TABLE loyalty_offers; -- due to schema mismatch
CREATE TABLE loyalty_offers (
                corporation_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                offer_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
                PRIMARY KEY (corporation_id, offer_id)
            );
CREATE INDEX idx_loyalty_offers_corporation_id 
            ON loyalty_offers(corporation_id)
        ;
